   # Parallel Development & Isolation Protocols
   > **STATUS: IGNORED BY DEFAULT.** You MUST NOT follow these instructions unless the human explicitly invokes
   parallel development, isolation protocols, or explicitly commands you to use a branch/PR workflow.

   To ensure safe parallel development across the team without merge conflicts or ODR (One Definition Rule) violations,
   you MUST adhere strictly to the following constraints for every code-generation task when this mode is invoked:

   1. **Git & Version Control Mandate:**
   - **Never commit to `main`.** You are strictly forbidden from pushing code directly to the `main` or `master`
   branch.
   - **Feature Branches:** Before writing a single line of code, use the GitHub CLI (`gh`) or standard `git` commands

   - **Pull Requests:** Upon completing Phase 3 (Performance) and verifying visual fidelity, commit your work to your
   branch and use the GitHub CLI to open a Pull Request against `main`.

   2. **Architectural Isolation (Single-Header Rule):**
   - **Self-Contained Code:** All new algorithms, geometries, or shaders MUST be encapsulated within a single `.h` file
   in the `include/` directory (or a highly specific `include/Alg/` subdirectory).
   - **No Cross-Pollination:** You may not `#include` any WIP headers being developed by other agents. Rely ONLY on
   standard library features, standard OpenGL/GLFW headers, and the locked, immutable core data structures (e.g.,
   `Alice::vec`, `AliceMemory::LinearArena`).
   - **Namespaces:** Wrap all your implementations in deeply nested namespaces to prevent collisions (e.g., `namespace
   Alice::Alg::[YourFeature]`).

   3. **Macro-Gated Unit Testing:**
   - **Do not permanently alter main loops.** When testing your algorithm in `src/sketch.cpp`, wrap your includes,
   initializations, and render calls within a unique preprocessor macro block.
   - **Format:** `#ifdef ALICE_TEST_[YOUR_FEATURE_NAME] ... #endif`. This ensures tests remain dormant upon merge
   unless explicitly defined.

  ✓  WriteFile  ApiKeyReader.h → Accepted (+50, -0)

       1 #ifndef ALICE_API_KEY_READER_H
       2 #define ALICE_API_KEY_READER_H
       3
       4 #include <fstream>
       5 #include <string>
       6 #include <cstring>
       7
       8 namespace Alice
       9 {
      10     struct ApiKeyReader
      11     {
      12         static bool GetGoogleKey(char* outBuffer, size_t bufferSize)
      13         {
      14             std::ifstream file("API_KEYS.txt");
      15             if (!file.is_open())
      16             {
      17                 return false;
      18             }
      19
      20             std::string line;
      21             const char* targetKey = "GOOGLE_API_KEY=";
      22             size_t targetLen = strlen(targetKey);
      23
      24             while (std::getline(file, line))
      25             {
      26                 if (line.compare(0, targetLen, targetKey) == 0)
      27                 {
      28                     std::string value = line.substr(targetLen);
      29                     // Trim potential whitespace or carriage returns from Windows
      30                     size_t end = value.find_last_not_of(" \r\n\t");
      31                     if (std::string::npos != end)
      32                     {
      33                         value = value.substr(0, end + 1);
      34                     }
      35
      36                     if (value.length() < bufferSize)
      37                     {
      38                         strncpy(outBuffer, value.c_str(), bufferSize);
      39                         outBuffer[bufferSize - 1] = '\0';
      40                         return true;
      41                     }
      42                 }
      43             }
      44
      45             return false;
      46         }
      47     };
      48 }
      49
      50 #endif // ALICE_API_KEY_READER_H

  allocations during the parsing loop, adhering strictly to Allman style and minimizing headers.


  ✓  WriteFile  ApiKeyReader.h → Accepted (+50, -0)

       1 #ifndef ALICE_API_KEY_READER_H
       2 #define ALICE_API_KEY_READER_H
       3
       4 #include <fstream>
       5 #include <string>
       6 #include <cstring>
       7
       8 namespace Alice
       9 {
      10     struct ApiKeyReader
      11     {
      12         static bool GetGoogleKey(char* outBuffer, size_t bufferSize)
      13         {
      14             std::ifstream file("API_KEYS.txt");
      15             if (!file.is_open())
      16             {
      17                 return false;
      18             }
      19
      20             std::string line;
      21             const char* targetKey = "GOOGLE_API_KEY=";
      22             size_t targetLen = strlen(targetKey);
      23
      24             while (std::getline(file, line))
      25             {
      26                 if (line.compare(0, targetLen, targetKey) == 0)
      27                 {
      28                     std::string value = line.substr(targetLen);
      29                     // Trim potential whitespace or carriage returns from Windows
      30                     size_t end = value.find_last_not_of(" \r\n\t");
      31                     if (std::string::npos != end)
      32                     {
      33                         value = value.substr(0, end + 1);
      34                     }
      35
      36                     if (value.length() < bufferSize)
      37                     {
      38                         strncpy(outBuffer, value.c_str(), bufferSize);
      39                         outBuffer[bufferSize - 1] = '\0';
      40                         return true;
      41                     }
      42                 }
      43             }
      44
      45             return false;
      46         }
      47     };
      48 }
      49
      50 #endif // ALICE_API_KEY_READER_H

✦ I will now create include/AliceNetwork.h to provide a generalized and reusable network fetching interface, abstracting
  the libcurl logic previously found in GLBLoader.h.


  ✓  WriteFile  AliceNetwork.h → Accepted (+59, -0)

       1 #ifndef ALICE_NETWORK_H
       2 #define ALICE_NETWORK_H
       3
       4 #include <curl/curl.h>
       5 #include <vector>
       6 #include <string>
       7 #include <cstdio>
       8 #include <cstring>
       9
      10 namespace Alice
      11 {
      12     struct Network
      13     {
      14         static size_t write_callback(void* contents, size_t size, size_t nmemb, void* userp)
      15         {
      16             size_t realsize = size * nmemb;
      17             std::vector<uint8_t>* mem = (std::vector<uint8_t>*)userp;
      18             size_t oldsize = mem->size();
      19             mem->resize(oldsize + realsize);
      20             memcpy(mem->data() + oldsize, contents, realsize);
      21             return realsize;
      22         }
      23
      24         static bool Fetch(const char* url, std::vector<uint8_t>& buffer)
      25         {
      26             std::string sUrl = url;
      27             if (sUrl.find("http://") == 0 || sUrl.find("https://") == 0)
      28             {
      29                 CURL* curl = curl_easy_init();
      30                 if (!curl) return false;
      31
      32                 curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_URL, url);
      33                 curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_WRITEFUNCTION, write_callback);
      34                 curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_WRITEDATA, (void*)&buffer);
      35                 curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_FOLLOWLOCATION, 1L);
      36                 curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_SSL_VERIFYPEER, 0L);
      37                 curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_USERAGENT, "AliceViewer/1.0");
      38
      39                 CURLcode res = curl_easy_perform(curl);
      40                 curl_easy_cleanup(curl);
      41                 return (res == CURLE_OK);
      42             }
      43             else
      44             {
      45                 FILE* f = fopen(url, "rb");
      46                 if (!f) return false;
      47                 fseek(f, 0, SEEK_END);
      48                 size_t size = ftell(f);
      49                 fseek(f, 0, SEEK_SET);
      50                 buffer.resize(size);
      51                 fread(buffer.data(), 1, size, f);
      52                 fclose(f);
      53                 return true;
      54             }
      55         }
      56     };
      57 }
      58
      59 #endif // ALICE_NETWORK_H

✦ I will now create include/AliceNetwork.h to provide a generalized and reusable network fetching interface, abstracting
  the libcurl logic previously found in GLBLoader.h.


  ✓  WriteFile  AliceNetwork.h → Accepted (+59, -0)

       1 #ifndef ALICE_NETWORK_H
       2 #define ALICE_NETWORK_H
       3
       4 #include <curl/curl.h>
       5 #include <vector>
       6 #include <string>
       7 #include <cstdio>
       8 #include <cstring>
       9
      10 namespace Alice
      11 {
      12     struct Network
      13     {
      14         static size_t write_callback(void* contents, size_t size, size_t nmemb, void* userp)
      15         {
      16             size_t realsize = size * nmemb;
      17             std::vector<uint8_t>* mem = (std::vector<uint8_t>*)userp;
      18             size_t oldsize = mem->size();
      19             mem->resize(oldsize + realsize);
      20             memcpy(mem->data() + oldsize, contents, realsize);
      21             return realsize;
      22         }
      23
      24         static bool Fetch(const char* url, std::vector<uint8_t>& buffer)
      25         {
      26             std::string sUrl = url;
      27             if (sUrl.find("http://") == 0 || sUrl.find("https://") == 0)
      28             {
      29                 CURL* curl = curl_easy_init();
      30                 if (!curl) return false;
      31
      32                 curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_URL, url);
      33                 curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_WRITEFUNCTION, write_callback);
      34                 curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_WRITEDATA, (void*)&buffer);
      35                 curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_FOLLOWLOCATION, 1L);
      36                 curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_SSL_VERIFYPEER, 0L);
      37                 curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_USERAGENT, "AliceViewer/1.0");
      38
      39                 CURLcode res = curl_easy_perform(curl);
      40                 curl_easy_cleanup(curl);
      41                 return (res == CURLE_OK);
      42             }
      43             else
      44             {
      45                 FILE* f = fopen(url, "rb");
      46                 if (!f) return false;
      47                 fseek(f, 0, SEEK_END);
      48                 size_t size = ftell(f);
      49                 fseek(f, 0, SEEK_SET);
      50                 buffer.resize(size);
      51                 fread(buffer.data(), 1, size, f);

   unless explicitly defined.

      151 +                 float p[3], n[3] = { 0,0,1 };
      152 +                 cgltf_accessor_read_float(pos_acc, i, p, 3);
      153 +                 if (norm_acc) cgltf_accessor_read_float(norm_acc, i, n, 3);
      154 +
      155 +                 // ECEF to ENU transformation to prevent jitter
      156 +                 double dx = (double)p[0] - centerEcef.x;
      157 +                 double dy = (double)p[1] - centerEcef.y;
      158 +                 double dz = (double)p[2] - centerEcef.z;
      159 +
      160 +                 float lx = (float)(enuMat[0] * dx + enuMat[1] * dy + enuMat[2] * dz);
      161 +                 float ly = (float)(enuMat[4] * dx + enuMat[5] * dy + enuMat[6] * dz);
      162 +                 float lz = (float)(enuMat[8] * dx + enuMat[9] * dy + enuMat[10] * dz);
      163 +
      164 +                 verts[i * 6 + 0] = lx; verts[i * 6 + 1] = ly; verts[i * 6 + 2] = lz;
      165 +
      166 +                 if (lx < out_min.x) out_min.x = lx;
      167 +                 if (ly < out_min.y) out_min.y = ly;
      168 +                 if (lz < out_min.z) out_min.z = lz;
      169 +                 if (lx > out_max.x) out_max.x = lx;
      170 +                 if (ly > out_max.y) out_max.y = ly;
      171 +                 if (lz > out_max.z) out_max.z = lz;
      172 +
      173 +                 // Rotate normals (only rotation part of ENU)
      174 +                 float nx = (float)(enuMat[0] * n[0] + enuMat[1] * n[1] + enuMat[2] * n[2]);
      175 +                 float ny = (float)(enuMat[4] * n[0] + enuMat[5] * n[1] + enuMat[6] * n[2]);
      176 +                 float nz = (float)(enuMat[8] * n[0] + enuMat[9] * n[1] + enuMat[10] * n[2]);
      177 +                 float ilen = 1.0f / sqrtf(nx * nx + ny * ny + nz * nz + 1e-12f);
      178 +                 verts[i * 6 + 3] = nx * ilen; verts[i * 6 + 4] = ny * ilen; verts[i * 6 + 5] = nz *
          ilen;
      179 +             }
      180 +
      181 +             size_t icount = prim->indices ? prim->indices->count : 0;
      182 +             unsigned int* indices = (unsigned int*)Alice::g_Arena.allocate(icount * sizeof(unsigned
          int));
      183 +             for (size_t i = 0; i < icount; ++i) indices[i] = (unsigned
          int)cgltf_accessor_read_index(prim->indices, i);
      184 +
      185 +             out_mesh.instanceVbo = 0;
      186 +             out_mesh.count = (int)icount;
      187 +             glGenVertexArrays(1, &out_mesh.vao);
      188 +             glGenBuffers(1, &out_mesh.vbo);
      189 +             glGenBuffers(1, &out_mesh.ebo);
      190 +             glBindVertexArray(out_mesh.vao);
      191 +             glBindBuffer(GL_ARRAY_BUFFER, out_mesh.vbo);
      192 +             glBufferData(GL_ARRAY_BUFFER, vcount * 6 * sizeof(float), verts, GL_STATIC_DRAW);
